\hypertarget{sample-only-few-seconds-of-the-data-to-work}{%
\section{Sample only few seconds of the data to
work}\label{sample-only-few-seconds-of-the-data-to-work}}

gpstime in the las and in the traj files is in seconds The gpstime in
the las file is the emission time (same as trajectory time), not the
impact time.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{fstsec }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FloatTok{1679488739.935013055801}
\CommentTok{\# 3 seconds}
\NormalTok{Cloud }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ Cloud[gpstime }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=}\NormalTok{ fstsec}\DecValTok{{-}3} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ gpstime}\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}=}\NormalTok{ fstsec]}
\NormalTok{Traj }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ Traj[gpstime }\SpecialCharTok{\textgreater{}=}\NormalTok{ fstsec}\DecValTok{{-}3} \SpecialCharTok{\&}\NormalTok{ gpstime}\SpecialCharTok{\textless{}=}\NormalTok{ fstsec]}

\FunctionTok{plot3d}\NormalTok{(Traj[,.(x, y,z)], }\AttributeTok{aspect=}\NormalTok{F) }
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\hypertarget{compute-the-unit-vectors-between-sensor-position-and-the-acquired-point}{%
\section{Compute the unit vectors between sensor position and the
acquired
point}\label{compute-the-unit-vectors-between-sensor-position-and-the-acquired-point}}

\hypertarget{for-shots-with-echo}{%
\subsection{For shots with echo}\label{for-shots-with-echo}}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Remove useless columns}
\NormalTok{Ring1 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ Ring1[,.(Ring, gpstime, X,Y,Z, Range)]}
\NormalTok{Traj }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ Traj[,.(gpstime, x,y,z)]}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

Emission point: A Acquired points coordinates : B -\textgreater{}
Compute the direction vector (AB) between the emission and the acquired
point.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Acquired points coordinates (B)}
\NormalTok{Xb }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ Ring1}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{X}
\NormalTok{Yb }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ Ring1}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Y}
\NormalTok{Zb }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ Ring1}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Z}

\CommentTok{\# Interpolate coordinates of the emission point (A) (in the traj) from coordinates before and after (= barycentric interpolation)}
\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(Traj}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{gpstime) }\CommentTok{\# 300}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## [1] 300
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\FunctionTok{length}\NormalTok{(Traj}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{x) }\CommentTok{\# 300}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}

\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## [1] 1679488740
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{Xa }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{approx}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{x =}\NormalTok{ Traj}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{gpstime, }\AttributeTok{y =}\NormalTok{ Traj}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{x , }\AttributeTok{xout =}\NormalTok{ Ring1}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{gpstime)}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y }\CommentTok{\# x : temps de la traj, xout : temps du cloud, $y pour avoir les coordonées x et non les temps}
\NormalTok{Ya }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{approx}\NormalTok{(Traj}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{gpstime, }\AttributeTok{y =}\NormalTok{ Traj}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y , Ring1}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{gpstime)}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y}
\NormalTok{Za }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{approx}\NormalTok{(Traj}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{gpstime, }\AttributeTok{y =}\NormalTok{ Traj}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{z , Ring1}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{gpstime)}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y}

\CommentTok{\# Compute the coordinates of the AB vector between the emission and the acquired point}
\NormalTok{vector\_coord }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.frame}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{x\_dir =}\NormalTok{ Xb}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{Xa,}
                           \AttributeTok{y\_dir =}\NormalTok{ Yb}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{Ya,}
                           \AttributeTok{z\_dir =}\NormalTok{ Zb}\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{Za) }\CommentTok{\# coordinates}

\CommentTok{\# Compute the norm of the direction vector (AB)}
\NormalTok{vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Distance }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sqrt}\NormalTok{(}
\NormalTok{  (vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{x\_dir)}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2} \SpecialCharTok{+}\NormalTok{ (vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y\_dir)}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2} \SpecialCharTok{+}\NormalTok{ (vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{z\_dir)}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2}
\NormalTok{) }
\CommentTok{\# Transform in direction vector of norm = 1}
\NormalTok{vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{x\_dir }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{x\_dir }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Distance}
\NormalTok{vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y\_dir }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y\_dir }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Distance}
\NormalTok{vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{z\_dir }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{z\_dir }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Distance}

\CommentTok{\# Add A (emission) coordinates in the table}
\NormalTok{vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{X0 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ Xa}
\NormalTok{vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Y0 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ Ya}
\NormalTok{vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Z0 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ Za}

\CommentTok{\# and associated time }
\NormalTok{vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{gpstime }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ Ring1}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{gpstime }
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\hypertarget{check-that-we-retreive-the-original-point-for-emission-point-direction-vector-and-distance}{%
\subsubsection{Check that we retreive the original point for emission
point, direction vector and
distance:}\label{check-that-we-retreive-the-original-point-for-emission-point-direction-vector-and-distance}}

Recalculer x,y,zb : à partir de x,y,zo : xb = x0 + xdir * distance pour
vérifier qu'on est bon

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{check\_B }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.frame}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{XB =}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{X0 }\SpecialCharTok{+}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{x\_dir }\SpecialCharTok{*}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Distance,}
                      \AttributeTok{YB =}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Y0 }\SpecialCharTok{+}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y\_dir }\SpecialCharTok{*}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Distance,}
                      \AttributeTok{ZB =}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Z0 }\SpecialCharTok{+}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{z\_dir }\SpecialCharTok{*}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Distance)}

\CommentTok{\# Check that we retreive the original point from emission point, direction vector and distance:}
\FunctionTok{all}\NormalTok{(check\_B}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{XB }\SpecialCharTok{{-}}\NormalTok{ Ring1}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{X }\SpecialCharTok{==} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}

\subsubsection{Retreive direction

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Interpolate coordinates of the emission point (A) (in the traj) for the gaps gpstime (shots without echo)}
\NormalTok{Xa }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{approx}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{x =}\NormalTok{ Traj}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{gpstime, }\AttributeTok{y =}\NormalTok{ Traj}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{x, }\AttributeTok{xout =}\NormalTok{ gpstime\_gaps)}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y }\CommentTok{\# x : temps de la traj, xout : temps des gaps, $y pour avoir les coordonées x et non les temps}
\NormalTok{Ya }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{approx}\NormalTok{(Traj}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{gpstime, }\AttributeTok{y =}\NormalTok{ Traj}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y , gpstime\_gaps)}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y}
\NormalTok{Za }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{approx}\NormalTok{(Traj}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{gpstime, }\AttributeTok{y =}\NormalTok{ Traj}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{z , gpstime\_gaps)}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y}

\CommentTok{\# Interpolate the direction vectors of this shots without echo (intercalate between vectors of the shots with echo)}
\NormalTok{x\_dir }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{approx}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{x =}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{gpstime, }\AttributeTok{y =}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{x\_dir, }\AttributeTok{xout =}\NormalTok{ gpstime\_gaps)}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y}
\NormalTok{y\_dir }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{approx}\NormalTok{(vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{gpstime, }\AttributeTok{y =}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y\_dir, gpstime\_gaps)}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y}
\NormalTok{z\_dir }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{approx}\NormalTok{(vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{gpstime, }\AttributeTok{y =}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{z\_dir, gpstime\_gaps)}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y}


\CommentTok{\# In a table:}
\NormalTok{gaps\_vector\_coord }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{data.frame}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{x\_dir =}\NormalTok{ x\_dir, }\CommentTok{\# vector coordinates}
                                \AttributeTok{y\_dir =}\NormalTok{ y\_dir,}
                                \AttributeTok{z\_dir =}\NormalTok{ z\_dir,}
                                \AttributeTok{Distance =} \DecValTok{100}\NormalTok{,}\CommentTok{\# m. Il n\textquotesingle{}y a pas de distance puisqu\textquotesingle{}il n\textquotesingle{}y a pas d\textquotesingle{}echo}
                                \AttributeTok{gpstime =}\NormalTok{ gpstime\_gaps) }

\CommentTok{\# Compute the norm of the direction vector}
\NormalTok{gaps\_dir\_norm }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{sqrt}\NormalTok{(gaps\_vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{x\_dir}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2} \SpecialCharTok{+}\NormalTok{ gaps\_vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y\_dir}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2} \SpecialCharTok{+}\NormalTok{ gaps\_vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{z\_dir}\SpecialCharTok{\^{}}\DecValTok{2}\NormalTok{)}\CommentTok{\# n\textquotesingle{}a pas conservé une norme =1}

\CommentTok{\# Transform in unit vector (norm = 1)}
\NormalTok{gaps\_vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{x\_dir }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ gaps\_vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{x\_dir }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ gaps\_dir\_norm}
\NormalTok{gaps\_vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y\_dir }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ gaps\_vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y\_dir }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ gaps\_dir\_norm}
\NormalTok{gaps\_vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{z\_dir }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ gaps\_vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{z\_dir }\SpecialCharTok{/}\NormalTok{ gaps\_dir\_norm}

\NormalTok{gaps\_vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{X0 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ Xa}
\NormalTok{gaps\_vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Y0 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ Ya}
\NormalTok{gaps\_vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Z0 }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}}\NormalTok{ Za}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\hypertarget{test-our-calcul-for-shots-without-echo}{%
\section{Test our calcul for shots without
echo}\label{test-our-calcul-for-shots-without-echo}}

To check if our calcul works, we can remove a part of known data and
check if we retrieve it : créer des faux sans écho We can remove: -
randomly 10\% of known data - a continuous part of known data We can
also quantified the error at 100 m : 1) avec le vecteur directeur on
projette les points à 100m (distance) 2) après je vire les 10\% (on fait
des faux sans écho) 3) après on essaye de les retouver les faux tirs
sans écho (on compare le Xb Initial à 100m et celui estimé à 100m)

If we retreive the removed points means that the sensor rotation speed
is stable.

\hypertarget{project-the-points-100-m-from-their-point-of-emission}{%
\subsection{Project the points 100 m from their point of
emission}\label{project-the-points-100-m-from-their-point-of-emission}}

Emission point (X,Y,Z0) + coord of the direction vector(x,y,z\_dir) *
Distance (100 m)

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{XB100 }\OtherTok{=}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{X0 }\SpecialCharTok{+}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{x\_dir }\SpecialCharTok{*} \DecValTok{100}
\NormalTok{vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{YB100 }\OtherTok{=}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Y0 }\SpecialCharTok{+}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{y\_dir }\SpecialCharTok{*} \DecValTok{100}
\NormalTok{vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{ZB100 }\OtherTok{=}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{Z0 }\SpecialCharTok{+}\NormalTok{ vector\_coord}\SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{z\_dir }\SpecialCharTok{*} \DecValTok{100}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\NormalTok{Test\_10Cloud[}\FunctionTok{sample}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(Test\_10Cloud), }\FloatTok{0.1} \SpecialCharTok{*} \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(Test\_10Cloud)), }\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"XB100"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"YB100"}\NormalTok{, }\StringTok{"ZB100"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{:}\ErrorTok{=} \ConstantTok{NA\_real\_}\NormalTok{]}
